TL;DR: 该论文解决了从有限、嘈杂的神经记录中推断跨任务神经动力学的挑战，提出了JEDI模型，通过共享嵌入空间学习实现了可扩展、可泛化的脑动力学推断，并在模拟数据和猴子运动皮层记录中验证了其有效性。
摘要翻译

动物大脑能够通过单一神经网络灵活高效地完成多种行为任务。现代神经科学的一个核心目标是将大脑灵活性的机制映射到神经群体活动的动力学基础上。然而，从有限、嘈杂且高维度的实验神经记录中识别出任务特异性的动力学规则仍然是一个重大挑战，因为实验数据通常只能部分反映大脑状态和动力学机制。虽然直接受神经数据约束的循环神经网络（RNN）在推断底层动力学机制方面已显示出有效性，但它们通常局限于单一任务领域，难以在不同行为条件下泛化。在此，我们提出JEDI这一分层模型，它通过在RNN权重上学习一个共享的嵌入空间，来捕捉跨任务和跨情境的神经动力学。该模型能够复现神经动力学的个体样本，同时可扩展至任意大规模复杂数据集，并在一个统一的模型中揭示不同条件间的共享结构。通过使用模拟的RNN数据集，我们证明JEDI能够准确学习到稳健、可泛化且具有条件特异性的嵌入表示。通过对JEDI学习到的权重进行逆向工程，我们表明该模型能够恢复真实的固定点结构，并在特征谱中揭示底层神经动力学的关键特征。最后，我们将JEDI应用于猴子伸手运动期间的皮层运动区记录，以提取关于运动控制神经动力学的机制性见解。我们的研究表明，情境嵌入与循环权重的联合学习，能够仅从神经记录中实现对大脑动力学的可扩展且可泛化的推断。

Abstract

Animal brains flexibly and efficiently achieve many behavioral tasks with a single neural network. A core goal in modern neuroscience is to map the mechanisms of the brain's flexibility onto the dynamics underlying neural populations. However, identifying task-specific dynamical rules from limited, noisy, and high-dimensional experimental neural recordings remains a major challenge, as experimental data often provide only partial access to brain states and dynamical mechanisms. While recurrent neural networks (RNNs) directly constrained neural data have been effective in inferring underlying dynamical mechanisms, they are typically limited to single-task domains and struggle to generalize across behavioral conditions. Here, we introduce JEDI, a hierarchical model that captures neural dynamics across tasks and contexts by learning a shared embedding space over RNN weights. This model recapitulates individual samples of neural dynamics while scaling to arbitrarily large and complex datasets, uncovering shared structure across conditions in a single, unified model. Using simulated RNN datasets, we demonstrate that JEDI accurately learns robust, generalizable, condition-specific embeddings. By reverse-engineering the weights learned by JEDI, we show that it recovers ground truth fixed point structures and unveils key features of the underlying neural dynamics in the eigenspectra. Finally, we apply JEDI to motor cortex recordings during monkey reaching to extract mechanistic insight into the neural dynamics of motor control. Our work shows that joint learning of contextual embeddings and recurrent weights provides scalable and generalizable inference of brain dynamics from recordings alone.

42. Dual Space Preconditioning for Gradient Descent in the Overparameterized Regime FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Reza Ghane, Danil Akhtiamov, Babak Hassibi
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了双空间预处理梯度下降在过参数化线性模型中的收敛性，证明了迭代总是收敛到满足数据拟合条件的解，并分析了不同预处理器的隐式偏差特性。
摘要翻译

本研究探讨了对偶空间预处理梯度下降法的收敛性质，该方法涵盖了归一化梯度下降、梯度裁剪及Adam等优化器。我们考虑形式为$\nabla K$的预处理算子，其中$K: \mathbb{R}^p \to \mathbb{R}$为凸函数，并假设该算子用于训练一个过参数化的线性模型，其损失函数形式为$\ell({X} {W} - {Y})$，权重${W} \in \mathbb{R}^{d \times k}$，标签${Y} \in \mathbb{R}^{n \times k}$，数据${X} \in \mathbb{R}^{n \times d}$。在上述假设下，我们证明预处理梯度下降的迭代序列始终收敛于满足${X}{W}_{\infty} = {Y}$的点${W}_{\infty} \in \mathbb{R}^{d \times k}$。我们的证明方法具有独立的理论价值，通过引入一种新形式的Bregman散度及其相关恒等式，从而建立了收敛性结论。此外，我们还研究了对偶空间预处理梯度下降的隐式偏差。首先，我们通过实验表明，对于一般的$K(\cdot)$，${W}_\infty$依赖于所选学习率，这阻碍了对隐式偏差的精确刻画。其次，对于形式为$K({G}) = h(\|{G}\|_F)$的预处理算子（称为\textit{各向同性预处理算子}），我们证明${W}_\infty$在满足${X}{W}_\infty = {Y}$的条件下最小化$\|{W}_\infty - {W}_0\|_F^2$，其中${W}_0$为初始化权重。记从${W}_0$初始化的梯度下降法的收敛点为${W}_{\text{GD}, \infty}$，我们指出对于各向同性预处理算子有${W}_{\infty} = {W}_{\text{GD}, \infty}$。最后，我们证明对于一般预处理算子，类似结论在乘法常数范围内成立，即存在常数$c>0$使得$\|{W}_0 - {W}_{\infty}\|_F \le c \|{W}_0 - {W}_{\text{GD}, \infty}\|_F$。

Abstract

In this work we study the convergence properties of the Dual Space Preconditioned Gradient Descent, encompassing optimizers such as Normalized Gradient Descent, Gradient Clipping and Adam. We consider preconditioners of the form $\nabla K$, where $K: \mathbb{R}^p \to \mathbb{R}$ is convex and assume that the latter is applied to train an over-parameterized linear model with loss of the form $\ell({X} {W} - {Y})$, for weights ${W} \in \mathbb{R}^{d \times k}$, labels ${Y} \in \mathbb{R}^{n \times k}$ and data ${X} \in \mathbb{R}^{n \times d}$. Under the aforementioned assumptions, we prove that the iterates of the preconditioned gradient descent always converge to a point ${W}_{\infty} \in \mathbb{R}^{d \times k}$ satisfying ${X}{W}_{\infty} = {Y}$. Our proof techniques are of independent interest as we introduce a novel version of the Bregman Divergence with accompanying identities that allow us to establish convergence. We also study the implicit bias of Dual Space Preconditioned Gradient Descent. First, we demonstrate empirically that, for general $K(\cdot)$, ${W}_\infty$ depends on the chosen learning rate, hindering a precise characterization of the implicit bias. Then, for preconditioners of the form $K({G}) = h(\|{G}\|_F)$, known as \textit{isotropic preconditioners}, we show that ${W}_\infty$ minimizes $\|{W}_\infty - {W}_0\|_F^2$ subject to ${X}{W}_\infty = {Y}$, where ${W}_0$ is the initialization. Denoting the convergence point of GD initialized at ${W}_0$ by ${W}_{\text{GD}, \infty}$, we thus note ${W}_{\infty} = {W}_{\text{GD}, \infty}$ for isotropic preconditioners. Finally, we show that a similar fact holds for general preconditioners up to a multiplicative constant, namely, $\|{W}_0 - {W}_{\infty}\|_F \le c \|{W}_0 - {W}_{\text{GD}, \infty}\|_F$ for a constant $c>0$.

43. Muscle Synergy Priors Enhance Biomechanical Fidelity in Predictive Musculoskeletal Locomotion Simulation FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Ilseung Park, Eunsik Choi, Jangwhan Ahn, Jooeun Ahn
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于肌肉协同的强化学习框架，用于提高预测性肌肉骨骼运动模拟的生物力学保真度和泛化能力，在有限实验数据下成功模拟了不同速度、坡度和地形条件下的稳定步态。
摘要翻译

人类运动产生于高维神经肌肉控制，这使得预测性肌肉骨骼仿真具有挑战性。我们提出了一种生理学启发的强化学习框架，该框架利用肌肉协同作用来约束控制。我们通过分析少量地面行走试验的逆向肌肉骨骼数据，提取了一个低维协同作用基，并将其用作一个肌肉驱动的三维模型的动作空间，该模型在多种速度、坡度和不平坦地形上进行了训练。由此产生的控制器能在0.7至1.8米/秒的速度范围内以及±6°的坡度上生成稳定的步态，并再现了关节角度、关节力矩和地面反作用力随条件变化的调节模式。与无约束的控制器相比，协同约束控制减少了非生理性的膝关节运动学特征，并使膝关节力矩曲线保持在实验数据包络之内。在各种条件下，仿真的垂直地面反作用力与人体测量数据高度相关，肌肉激活时序也基本落在受试者间的变异范围之内。这些结果表明，将神经生理学结构嵌入强化学习中，能够利用有限的实验数据，提高预测性人类运动仿真的生物力学保真度和泛化能力。

Abstract

Human locomotion emerges from high-dimensional neuromuscular control, making predictive musculoskeletal simulation challenging. We present a physiology-informed reinforcement-learning framework that constrains control using muscle synergies. We extracted a low-dimensional synergy basis from inverse musculoskeletal analyses of a small set of overground walking trials and used it as the action space for a muscle-driven three-dimensional model trained across variable speeds, slopes and uneven terrain. The resulting controller generated stable gait from 0.7-1.8 m/s and on $\pm$ 6$^{\circ}$ grades and reproduced condition-dependent modulation of joint angles, joint moments and ground reaction forces. Compared with an unconstrained controller, synergy-constrained control reduced non-physiological knee kinematics and kept knee moment profiles within the experimental envelope. Across conditions, simulated vertical ground reaction forces correlated strongly with human measurements, and muscle-activation timing largely fell within inter-subject variability. These results show that embedding neurophysiological structure into reinforcement learning can improve biomechanical fidelity and generalization in predictive human locomotion simulation with limited experimental data.

44. Beam-Plasma Collective Oscillations in Intense Charged-Particle Beams: Dielectric Response Theory, Langmuir Wave Dispersion, and Unsupervised Detection via Prometheus FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Brandon Yee, Wilson Collins, Michael Iofin, Jiayi Fu
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了中等能量（10-100 MeV）强流带电粒子束中的束流-等离子体集体振荡，通过理论推导和基于beta-VAE的无监督检测方法，证明了朗缪尔波模式的存在性、等离子体频率的分布无关性，并验证了密度可调的等离子体共振等预测特征。
摘要翻译

我们针对中等能量（10-100 MeV）强流带电粒子束中的束-等离子体集体振荡，建立了一套理论与计算框架。在第一部分，我们构建了由弗拉索夫-泊松系统支配的动理学场论，推导了适用于三种束分布函数的林哈德介电函数与随机相位近似极化张量。通过介电函数 epsilon(omega,q)=0，我们证明了在临界束密度 n_c 以上存在无阻尼的朗缪尔波模式，获得了显式的束-等离子体色散关系，并证明了朗道阻尼在粒子-空穴连续谱之上消失。等离子体频率 Omega_p^2 = ne^2/(m*epsilon_0) 由 f-求和规则确定，与分布形状无关；更高阶的色散系数则依赖于速度矩。空间电荷效应驱动了以 sqrt(n-n_c) 起始的异常束流展宽，并在 q=2k_F 处产生弗里德尔振荡。通过重正化群分析，束-等离子体转变属于三维伊辛普适类。在第二部分，我们使用 Prometheus（一种在粒子网格法束模拟的静态结构因子数据 S(q) 上训练的 beta-变分自编码器）验证了这些预测。Prometheus 检测到高斯分布与均匀分布中集体等离子体振荡的起始，确认其在简并费米气体（n_c -> 0）中不存在，并解析了 q=2k_F 处的科恩异常。对粒子网格法模拟得到的 S(q,omega) 进行的色散分析，验证了由 f-求和规则预测的、与分布无关的 Omega_p。全部六项验证检查均通过。所预测的特征——频率 omega_p 正比于 sqrt(n) 且密度可调的等离子体共振、以 sqrt(n-n_c) 起始的异常束流展宽以及弗里德尔振荡——在现有的中等能量束流装置上均可观测。

Abstract

We develop a theoretical and computational framework for beam-plasma collective oscillations in intense charged-particle beams at intermediate energies (10-100 MeV). In Part I, we formulate a kinetic field theory governed by the Vlasov-Poisson system, deriving the Lindhard dielectric function and random phase approximation (RPA) polarization tensor for three beam distribution functions. We prove via the dielectric function epsilon(omega,q)=0 the existence of undamped Langmuir wave modes above a critical beam density n_c, obtain explicit beam-plasma dispersion relations, and show that Landau damping vanishes above the particle-hole continuum. The plasma frequency Omega_p^2 = ne^2/(m*epsilon_0) is fixed by the f-sum rule independently of distribution shape; higher dispersion coefficients depend on velocity moments. Space charge effects drive anomalous beam broadening with sqrt(n-n_c) onset and Friedel oscillations at q=2k_F. The beam-plasma transition belongs to the 3D Ising universality class via renormalization group analysis. In Part II, we validate these predictions using Prometheus, a beta-VAE trained on static structure factor data S(q) from particle-in-cell (PIC) beam simulations. Prometheus detects collective plasma oscillation onset in Gaussian and uniform distributions, confirms their absence in the degenerate Fermi gas (n_c -> 0), and resolves the Kohn anomaly at q=2k_F. Dispersion analysis of S(q,omega) from PIC simulations verifies the distribution-independent Omega_p predicted by the f-sum rule. All six validation checks pass. Predicted signatures -- density-tunable plasma resonances at omega_p proportional to sqrt(n), anomalous beam broadening with sqrt(n-n_c) onset, and Friedel oscillations -- are accessible at existing intermediate-energy beam facilities.

摘要翻译

本研究提出一种多分辨率卷积长短期记忆网络集成框架，该框架利用多样化的时间输入分辨率来减少误差累积，并提升分阶段开挖过程中支挡结构行为的长期预测性能。通过PLAXIS2D数值模拟构建了包含五层土层结构、两种开挖深度（14米与20米）以及随机变化岩土与结构参数的大规模侧向墙体位移响应数据库，生成了2000组时序变形曲线。三个在不同输入分辨率下训练的ConvLSTM模型通过全连接神经网络元学习器进行集成，构建出集成预测模型。基于数值结果与现场实测数据的验证表明，该集成方法在预测性能上持续优于单一ConvLSTM模型，尤其在长期多步预测中表现出更低的误差传播和更强的泛化能力。这些发现凸显了多分辨率集成策略在人工智能驱动的岩土工程预测中的潜力，该策略通过协同利用多时间尺度输入信息，有效提升了预测的稳定性与准确性。

Abstract

This study proposes a multi-resolution Convolutional Long Short-Term Memory (ConvLSTM) ensemble framework that leverages diverse temporal input resolutions to mitigate error accumulation and improve long-horizon forecasting of retaining-structure behavior during staged excavation. An extensive database of lateral wall displacement responses was generated through PLAXIS2D simulations incorporating five-layered soil stratigraphy, two excavation depths (14 and 20 m), and stochastically varied geotechnical and structural parameters, yielding 2,000 time-series deflection profiles. Three ConvLSTM models trained at different input resolutions were integrated using a fully connected neural network meta-learner to construct the ensemble model. Validation using both numerical results and field measurements demonstrated that the ensemble approach consistently outperformed the standalone ConvLSTM models, particularly in long-term multi-step prediction, exhibiting reduced error propagation and improved generalization. These findings underscore the potential of multi-resolution ensemble strategies that jointly exploit diverse temporal input scales to enhance predictive stability and accuracy in AI-driven geotechnical forecasting.

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于最优传输理论的多输出保序回归方法（Brenier保序回归），用于处理循环单调性约束的回归问题，并在概率校准任务中表现出优于基线的鲁棒性能。
摘要翻译

等渗回归（Isotonic Regression，IR）是一种形状约束回归方法，旨在保持单变量拟合曲线的非递减特性，其在单指标模型和概率校准等领域具有广泛应用。然而，在多输出回归问题中，经典等渗回归不再适用，因为单调性无法直接推广。本文研究一种新颖的多输出回归问题，其中回归函数需满足\emph{循环单调性}。简而言之，循环单调函数是某个凸势能的梯度。尽管强制实现循环单调性具有明显挑战，我们利用康托罗维奇最优传输（Optimal Transport，OT）理论中一个关键性质：最优解总是产生循环单调耦合。这一视角使我们能够自然地将回归函数和凸势能分别解释为广义线性模型中的连接函数以及最优传输中的布雷尼尔势能，因此我们将这一等渗回归的扩展称为\emph{布雷尼尔等渗回归}。我们通过概率校准和广义线性模型进行了实验验证。特别地，在概率校准任务中，等渗回归方法稳健地优于多种著名基线模型。

Abstract

Isotonic regression (IR) is shape-constrained regression to maintain a univariate fitting curve non-decreasing, which has numerous applications including single-index models and probability calibration. When it comes to multi-output regression, the classical IR is no longer applicable because the monotonicity is not readily extendable. We consider a novel multi-output regression problem where a regression function is \emph{cyclically monotone}. Roughly speaking, a cyclically monotone function is the gradient of some convex potential. Whereas enforcing cyclic monotonicity is apparently challenging, we leverage the fact that Kantorovich's optimal transport (OT) always yields a cyclically monotone coupling as an optimal solution. This perspective naturally allows us to interpret a regression function and the convex potential as a link function in generalized linear models and Brenier's potential in OT, respectively, and hence we call this IR extension \emph{Brenier isotonic regression}. We demonstrate experiments with probability calibration and generalized linear models. In particular, IR outperforms many famous baselines in probability calibration robustly.

47. The Curse and Blessing of Mean Bias in FP4-Quantized LLM Training FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Hengjie Cao, Zhendong Huang, Mengyi Chen, Yifeng Yang, Fanqi Yu, Ruijun Huang, Fang Dong, Xin Zhang, Jixian Zhou, Anrui Chen, Mingzhi Dong, Yujiang Wang, Jinlong Hou, Qin Lv, Yuan Cheng, Tun Lu, Fan Yang, Li Shang
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究发现大语言模型在FP4量化训练中的数值不稳定性主要由秩一的均值偏差驱动，并提出通过简单的均值减法操作来消除这种偏差，从而显著缩小与BF16训练的损失差距并恢复下游性能。
摘要翻译

在自然语言上训练的大语言模型表现出显著的各向异性：少数方向集中了不成比例的能量，而其余维度则形成一个宽阔的语义尾部。在低比特训练机制中，这种几何结构变得数值不稳定。由于分块量化尺度由极端的元素级幅度决定，主导方向拉伸了动态范围，将长尾语义变化压缩至狭窄的数值区间内。我们证明，这种不稳定性主要由一个相干的一阶均值偏差驱动，该偏差构成了大语言模型表示中谱各向异性的主导成分。这一均值成分在模型各层和训练阶段中系统地出现，并构成了极端激活幅度的主要部分，使其成为低精度下动态范围膨胀的主要驱动因素。关键在于，由于主导的不稳定性是一阶的，它可以通过简单的源级均值减法操作来消除。这种以偏差为中心的调节方法，在仅需规约操作和标准量化内核的情况下，恢复了基于奇异值分解的谱方法所带来的大部分稳定性优势。在FP4（W4A4G4）训练上的实证结果表明，均值移除显著缩小了与BF16的损失差距，并恢复了下游任务性能，为稳定的低比特大语言模型训练提供了一条硬件高效的路径。

Abstract

Large language models trained on natural language exhibit pronounced anisotropy: a small number of directions concentrate disproportionate energy, while the remaining dimensions form a broad semantic tail. In low-bit training regimes, this geometry becomes numerically unstable. Because blockwise quantization scales are determined by extreme elementwise magnitudes, dominant directions stretch the dynamic range, compressing long-tail semantic variation into narrow numerical bins. We show that this instability is primarily driven by a coherent rank-one mean bias, which constitutes the dominant component of spectral anisotropy in LLM representations. This mean component emerges systematically across layers and training stages and accounts for the majority of extreme activation magnitudes, making it the principal driver of dynamic-range inflation under low precision. Crucially, because the dominant instability is rank-one, it can be eliminated through a simple source-level mean-subtraction operation. This bias-centric conditioning recovers most of the stability benefits of SVD-based spectral methods while requiring only reduction operations and standard quantization kernels. Empirical results on FP4 (W4A4G4) training show that mean removal substantially narrows the loss gap to BF16 and restores downstream performance, providing a hardware-efficient path to stable low-bit LLM training.

48. GGMPs: Generalized Gaussian Mixture Processes FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Vardaan Tekriwal, Mark D. Risser, Hengrui Luo, Marcus M. Noack
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于高斯过程的广义高斯混合过程（GGMP）方法，用于解决多模态、异方差和非高斯条件下的条件密度估计问题，并在合成和真实数据集上展示了其改进的分布近似能力。
摘要翻译

条件密度估计因多模态性、异方差性和强非高斯性而变得复杂。高斯过程（Gaussian Processes，GPs）提供了一个具有校准不确定性的原则性非参数框架，但标准GP回归受限于其单模态高斯预测形式。本文提出广义高斯混合过程（Generalized Gaussian Mixture Process，GGMP），这是一种基于GP的方法，用于在多模态条件密度估计场景中处理每个输入可能对应复杂输出分布（而非单一标量响应）的问题。GGMP结合了局部高斯混合拟合、跨输入分量对齐以及各分量异方差GP训练，以生成闭式高斯混合预测密度。该方法计算可行，兼容标准GP求解器与可扩展方法，并避免了朴素多模态GP公式中指数级增长的隐分配结构。实验表明，在具有显著非高斯性和多模态性的合成及真实数据集上，GGMP改善了分布近似效果。

Abstract

Conditional density estimation is complicated by multimodality, heteroscedasticity, and strong non-Gaussianity. Gaussian processes (GPs) provide a principled nonparametric framework with calibrated uncertainty, but standard GP regression is limited by its unimodal Gaussian predictive form. We introduce the Generalized Gaussian Mixture Process (GGMP), a GP-based method for multimodal conditional density estimation in settings where each input may be associated with a complex output distribution rather than a single scalar response. GGMP combines local Gaussian mixture fitting, cross-input component alignment and per-component heteroscedastic GP training to produce a closed-form Gaussian mixture predictive density. The method is tractable, compatible with standard GP solvers and scalable methods, and avoids the exponentially large latent-assignment structure of naive multimodal GP formulations. Empirically, GGMPs improve distributional approximation on synthetic and real-world datasets with pronounced non-Gaussianity and multimodality.

摘要翻译

用于回归任务的主动学习通过选择信息量最大的样本来降低标注成本。改进型贪婪采样是一种重要方法，它采用静态的乘法规则来平衡特征空间多样性与输出空间不确定性。本文提出加权改进型贪婪采样方法，该框架以动态的加法准则替代原有机制。我们将权重选择问题构建为强化学习任务，使智能体能够在整个学习过程中自适应调整探索与利用的平衡。在18个基准数据集和合成环境上的实验表明，WiGS在预测精度和标注效率上均优于iGS及其他基线方法，尤其在数据密度分布不规则的领域中，基线方法的乘法规则会忽略密集区域的高误差样本。

Abstract

Active learning for regression reduces labeling costs by selecting the most informative samples. Improved Greedy Sampling is a prominent method that balances feature-space diversity and output-space uncertainty using a static, multiplicative rule. We propose Weighted improved Greedy Sampling (WiGS), which replaces this framework with a dynamic, additive criterion. We formulate weight selection as a reinforcement learning problem, enabling an agent to adapt the exploration-investigation balance throughout learning. Experiments on 18 benchmark datasets and a synthetic environment show WiGS outperforms iGS and other baseline methods in both accuracy and labeling efficiency, particularly in domains with irregular data density where the baseline's multiplicative rule ignores high-error samples in dense regions.

50. Effective Dataset Distillation for Spatio-Temporal Forecasting with Bi-dimensional Compression FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Taehyung Kwon, Yeonje Choi, Yeongho Kim, Kijung Shin
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 本文针对时空时间序列预测中数据集过大导致训练成本高的问题，提出了首个双向压缩的时空数据集蒸馏方法STemDist，在五个真实数据集上实现了最高6倍训练加速、8倍内存节省和12%预测误差降低。
摘要翻译

时空时间序列在现实世界应用中广泛使用，包括交通预测和天气预报。它们是在长时间跨度和多个地点上观测得到的序列，天然表现为多维数据。预测是时空分析的核心任务，已有大量深度学习方法被开发用于解决该问题。然而，随着实践中数据集规模和模型复杂度的持续增长，训练深度学习模型已变得日益耗时且资源密集。针对这一挑战，一种有前景的解决方案是数据集蒸馏，它通过合成紧凑的数据集来有效替代原始数据用于模型训练。尽管在包括时间序列分析在内的多个领域取得了成功，但现有的数据集蒸馏方法仅压缩单一维度，这使得它们不太适用于时空数据集，因为其庞大的数据量是由空间和时间维度共同作用形成的。为克服这一局限，我们提出了STemDist，这是首个专用于时空时间序列预测的数据集蒸馏方法。我们方法的一个核心理念是以平衡的方式同时压缩时间和空间维度，从而减少训练时间和内存占用。我们进一步通过在集群层面而非单个位置层面进行蒸馏来降低蒸馏成本，并辅以基于子集的细粒度蒸馏技术来提升预测性能。在五个真实世界数据集上的实验表明，与通用及时间序列数据集蒸馏方法相比，通过我们的STemDist方法蒸馏得到的数据集能使模型训练（1）更快（最高达6倍）、（2）内存效率更高（最高达8倍），且（3）更有效（预测误差降低最高达12%）。

Abstract

Spatio-temporal time series are widely used in real-world applications, including traffic prediction and weather forecasting. They are sequences of observations over extensive periods and multiple locations, naturally represented as multidimensional data. Forecasting is a central task in spatio-temporal analysis, and numerous deep learning methods have been developed to address it. However, as dataset sizes and model complexities continue to grow in practice, training deep learning models has become increasingly time- and resource-intensive. A promising solution to this challenge is dataset distillation, which synthesizes compact datasets that can effectively replace the original data for model training. Although successful in various domains, including time series analysis, existing dataset distillation methods compress only one dimension, making them less suitable for spatio-temporal datasets, where both spatial and temporal dimensions jointly contribute to the large data volume. To address this limitation, we propose STemDist, the first dataset distillation method specialized for spatio-temporal time series forecasting. A key idea of our solution is to compress both temporal and spatial dimensions in a balanced manner, reducing training time and memory. We further reduce the distillation cost by performing distillation at the cluster level rather than the individual location level, and we complement this coarse-grained approach with a subset-based granular distillation technique that enhances forecasting performance. On five real-world datasets, we show empirically that, compared to both general and time-series dataset distillation methods, datasets distilled by our STemDist method enable model training (1) faster (up to 6X) (2) more memory-efficient (up to 8X), and (3) more effective (with up to 12% lower prediction error).

51. Designing Service Systems from Textual Evidence FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Ruicheng Ao, Hongyu Chen, Siyang Gao, Hanwei Li, David Simchi-Levi
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究如何利用有偏差的大语言模型评估文本证据来优化服务系统配置，同时通过选择性人工审核最小化成本，并开发了PP-LUCB算法在客户支持任务中实现90%的审核成本降低。
摘要翻译

设计服务系统需要在多种配置方案中进行选择——例如选择最佳的聊天机器人版本、最优的路由策略或最有效的质量控制程序。在许多服务系统中，性能质量的主要证据是文本形式的（如客户支持记录、投诉描述、合规审查报告），而非经典优化方法所假设的标量测量数据。大语言模型（LLMs）能够解读此类文本证据并生成标准化的质量评分，但这些自动化评估器存在系统性偏差，且偏差程度因不同方案和评估实例而异。人类专家评审虽保持准确但成本高昂。本研究探讨如何在自动化评估廉价但存在偏差的前提下，以高置信度确定最优服务配置，同时最小化昂贵的人工审核成本。我们将此问题形式化为一个序列决策问题：每次评估可获得存在偏差的代理评分，而经过验证的真实结果可通过额外成本选择性获取。我们证明，在偏差随方案变化的情况下，仅依赖LLM的选择策略会失效，且简单的选择性审核估计量可能产生渐近偏差。我们开发了一种结合代理评分与逆概率加权残差的估计量，并构建了任意时间有效的置信序列。所提出的PP-LUCB算法能联合决策需要评估的方案以及是否请求人工审核，将审核资源集中在LLM评估器可靠性最低的环节。我们证明了算法的正确性，并建立了依赖具体实例的成本边界，表明其具有接近最优的效率。在客户支持工单分类任务中，该算法在40次试验中均能正确识别最佳模型，同时实现了90%的审核成本降低。

Abstract

Designing service systems requires selecting among alternative configurations -- choosing the best chatbot variant, the optimal routing policy, or the most effective quality control procedure. In many service systems, the primary evidence of performance quality is textual -- customer support transcripts, complaint narratives, compliance review reports -- rather than the scalar measurements assumed by classical optimization methods. Large language models (LLMs) can read such textual evidence and produce standardized quality scores, but these automated judges exhibit systematic biases that vary across alternatives and evaluation instances. Human expert review remains accurate but costly. We study how to identify the best service configuration with high confidence while minimizing expensive human audits, given that automated evaluation is cheap but biased. We formalize this as a sequential decision problem where a biased proxy score is observed for every evaluation, and a verified outcome can be acquired selectively at additional cost. We prove that LLM-only selection fails under arm-dependent bias, and that naive selective-audit estimators can be asymptotically biased. We develop an estimator combining proxy scores with inverse-propensity-weighted residuals and construct anytime-valid confidence sequences. Our algorithm, PP-LUCB, jointly decides which alternatives to evaluate and whether to request human audits, concentrating reviews where the LLM judge is least reliable. We prove correctness and establish instance-dependent cost bounds showing near-optimal efficiency. On a customer support ticket classification task, our algorithm correctly identifies the best model in 40/40 trials while achieving 90\% audit cost reduction.

52. On the Learning Dynamics of Two-layer Linear Networks with Label Noise SGD FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Tongcheng Zhang, Zhanpeng Zhou, Mingze Wang, Andi Han, Wei Huang, Taiji Suzuki, Junchi Yan
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了带有标签噪声的随机梯度下降（SGD）在两层过参数化线性网络中的学习动态，揭示了从惰性训练到丰富训练的两阶段学习行为，并解释了标签噪声如何促进模型泛化。
摘要翻译

深度学习成功的关键因素之一在于基于梯度的训练算法中固有噪声所诱导的隐式偏好。受带标签噪声训练能提升模型泛化能力的实证观察启发，我们深入探究了带标签噪声的随机梯度下降（SGD）背后的内在机制。聚焦于一个两层过参数化线性网络，我们分析了标签噪声SGD的学习动态，揭示了一种两阶段学习行为。在**第一阶段**，模型权重的幅度逐渐减小，模型逃离惰性区域，进入丰富区域。在**第二阶段**，模型权重与真实插值器之间的对齐度增加，模型最终收敛。我们的分析强调了标签噪声在驱动从惰性区域向丰富区域转变中的关键作用，并初步解释了其经验上的成功。此外，我们将这些见解拓展至锐度感知最小化（Sharpness-Aware Minimization, SAM），表明支配标签噪声SGD的原理同样适用于更广泛的优化算法。在合成与真实场景下进行的大量实验有力地支持了我们的理论。代码发布于 https://github.com/a-usually/Label-Noise-SGD。

Abstract

One crucial factor behind the success of deep learning lies in the implicit bias induced by noise inherent in gradient-based training algorithms. Motivated by empirical observations that training with noisy labels improves model generalization, we delve into the underlying mechanisms behind stochastic gradient descent (SGD) with label noise. Focusing on a two-layer over-parameterized linear network, we analyze the learning dynamics of label noise SGD, unveiling a two-phase learning behavior. In \emph{Phase I}, the magnitudes of model weights progressively diminish, and the model escapes the lazy regime; enters the rich regime. In \emph{Phase II}, the alignment between model weights and the ground-truth interpolator increases, and the model eventually converges. Our analysis highlights the critical role of label noise in driving the transition from the lazy to the rich regime and minimally explains its empirical success. Furthermore, we extend these insights to Sharpness-Aware Minimization (SAM), showing that the principles governing label noise SGD also apply to broader optimization algorithms. Extensive experiments, conducted under both synthetic and real-world setups, strongly support our theory. Our code is released at https://github.com/a-usually/Label-Noise-SGD.

53. Graph-GRPO: Training Graph Flow Models with Reinforcement Learning FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Baoheng Zhu, Deyu Bo, Delvin Ce Zhang, Xiao Wang
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为Graph-GRPO的在线强化学习框架，用于训练图流模型（graph flow models），以更好地对齐复杂的人类偏好或任务特定目标，并在分子优化任务上实现了最先进的性能。
摘要翻译

图生成是一项具有广泛应用的基础任务，例如药物发现领域。近年来，基于离散流匹配的图生成方法——即图流模型（Graph Flow Model, GFM）——因其优越的性能和灵活的采样能力而崭露头角。然而，如何有效地将GFM与复杂的人类偏好或任务特定目标对齐，仍然是一个重大挑战。本文提出Graph-GRPO，一种在可验证奖励下训练GFM的在线强化学习（Reinforcement Learning, RL）框架。我们的方法做出了两个关键贡献：（1）我们推导出GFM转移概率的解析表达式，替代了蒙特卡洛采样，从而为RL训练实现了完全可微的轨迹展开；（2）我们提出一种优化策略，通过随机扰动图中的特定节点和边并重新生成它们，实现了对生成质量的局部探索与自我提升。在合成数据集和真实数据集上进行的大量实验验证了Graph-GRPO的有效性。仅使用50步去噪步骤，我们的方法在平面图和树图数据集上分别达到了95.0%和97.5%的有效-唯一-新颖性（Valid-Unique-Novelty）分数。此外，Graph-GRPO在分子优化任务中取得了最先进的性能，超越了基于图和基于片段的RL方法以及经典的遗传算法。

Abstract

Graph generation is a fundamental task with broad applications, such as drug discovery. Recently, discrete flow matching-based graph generation, \aka, graph flow model (GFM), has emerged due to its superior performance and flexible sampling. However, effectively aligning GFMs with complex human preferences or task-specific objectives remains a significant challenge. In this paper, we propose Graph-GRPO, an online reinforcement learning (RL) framework for training GFMs under verifiable rewards. Our method makes two key contributions: (1) We derive an analytical expression for the transition probability of GFMs, replacing the Monte Carlo sampling and enabling fully differentiable rollouts for RL training; (2) We propose a refinement strategy that randomly perturbs specific nodes and edges in a graph, and regenerates them, allowing for localized exploration and self-improvement of generation quality. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of Graph-GRPO. With only 50 denoising steps, our method achieves 95.0\% and 97.5\% Valid-Unique-Novelty scores on the planar and tree datasets, respectively. Moreover, Graph-GRPO achieves state-of-the-art performance on the molecular optimization tasks, outperforming graph-based and fragment-based RL methods as well as classic genetic algorithms.

Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 本文研究了Mixture-of-Experts模型中专家层与注意力层之间的最优计算分配比例，发现该比例与总计算量和模型稀疏度存在幂律关系，并提出了一个明确的公式来指导MoE模型的高效设计。
摘要翻译

本文提出了一种针对混合专家模型（Mixture-of-Experts, MoE）的神经缩放定律新扩展，重点关注专家子层与注意力子层之间的计算资源最优分配。随着MoE架构成为一种在不按比例增加计算量的前提下扩展模型容量的高效方法，确定专家层与注意力层之间的最优计算比例变得至关重要。我们将比例$r$定义为每个词元的总浮点运算次数中分配给专家层相对于注意力层的比例，并探究该比例如何与总体计算预算及模型稀疏性相互作用。通过对GPT风格的MoE Transformer模型进行大量实验，我们通过经验发现最优比例$r^*$与总计算量呈幂律关系，并随稀疏度变化。我们的分析推导出了$r^*$的显式公式，从而能够对专家-注意力计算分配进行精确控制。通过引入这一架构参数，我们推广了Chinchilla缩放定律，为在模型规模和数据之外调整MoE模型提供了一个新框架。我们的研究结果为设计高效的MoE模型提供了实用指导，可在固定计算预算内优化模型性能。

Abstract

This paper presents a novel extension of neural scaling laws to Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models, focusing on the optimal allocation of compute between expert and attention sub-layers. As MoE architectures have emerged as an efficient method for scaling model capacity without proportionally increasing computation, determining the optimal expert-attention compute ratio becomes critical. We define the ratio $r$ as the fraction of total FLOPs per token dedicated to the expert layers versus the attention layers, and explore how this ratio interacts with the overall compute budget and model sparsity. Through extensive experiments with GPT-style MoE Transformers, we empirically find that the optimal ratio $r^*$ follows a power-law relationship with total compute and varies with sparsity. Our analysis leads to an explicit formula for $r^*$, enabling precise control over the expert-attention compute allocation. We generalize the Chinchilla scaling law by incorporating this architectural parameter, providing a new framework for tuning MoE models beyond size and data. Our findings offer practical guidelines for designing efficient MoE models, optimizing performance while respecting fixed compute budgets.

55. Causal Concept Graphs in LLM Latent Space for Stepwise Reasoning FAIL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在大型语言模型潜在空间中构建因果概念图的方法，用于改进多步推理的可解释性，并在多个推理基准测试中验证了其有效性。
摘要翻译

稀疏自编码器能够定位概念在语言模型中的位置，但无法揭示其在多步推理过程中如何相互作用。我们提出因果概念图（Causal Concept Graphs, CCG）：一种基于稀疏可解释潜在特征的有向无环图，其边能够捕捉概念间习得的因果依赖关系。我们将面向任务的条件稀疏自编码器用于概念发现，并结合DAGMA风格的可微分结构学习进行图结构恢复，同时引入因果保真度评分（Causal Fidelity Score, CFS）以评估图引导的干预是否比随机干预产生更大的下游效应。在GPT-2 Medium模型上对ARC-Challenge、StrategyQA和LogiQA进行实验，经过五个随机种子（共15组配对运行）的测试，CCG取得了CFS=5.654±0.625的结果，优于ROME风格的追踪方法（3.382±0.233）、仅使用稀疏自编码器的排序方法（2.479±0.196）以及随机基线（1.032±0.034），且经Bonferroni校正后显著性达到p<0.0001。学习得到的图具有稀疏性（边密度5-6%）、领域特异性，并在不同随机种子间保持稳定。

Abstract

Sparse autoencoders can localize where concepts live in language models, but not how they interact during multi-step reasoning. We propose Causal Concept Graphs (CCG): a directed acyclic graph over sparse, interpretable latent features, where edges capture learned causal dependencies between concepts. We combine task-conditioned sparse autoencoders for concept discovery with DAGMA-style differentiable structure learning for graph recovery and introduce the Causal Fidelity Score (CFS) to evaluate whether graph-guided interventions induce larger downstream effects than random ones. On ARC-Challenge, StrategyQA, and LogiQA with GPT-2 Medium, across five seeds ($n{=}15$ paired runs), CCG achieves $\CFS=5.654\pm0.625$, outperforming ROME-style tracing ($3.382\pm0.233$), SAE-only ranking ($2.479\pm0.196$), and a random baseline ($1.032\pm0.034$), with $p<0.0001$ after Bonferroni correction. Learned graphs are sparse (5-6\% edge density), domain-specific, and stable across seeds.

56. HEAL: Hindsight Entropy-Assisted Learning for Reasoning Distillation FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Wenjing Zhang, Jiangze Yan, Jieyun Huang, Yi Shen, Shuming Shi, Ping Chen, Ning Wang, Zhaoxiang Liu, Kai Wang, Shiguo Lian
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文提出了HEAL框架，通过熵辅助修复、严格过滤和渐进式课程学习，解决了从大型推理模型向小型模型蒸馏推理能力时因教师模型能力限制而产生的“教师天花板”问题，并在多个基准测试中显著超越了传统蒸馏方法。
摘要翻译

将大型推理模型（LRMs）的推理能力蒸馏至较小模型通常受限于拒绝采样的约束。传统方法将教师模型视为静态过滤器，丢弃教师无法独立探索有效解决方案的复杂“边缘案例”问题，从而为学生模型人为设置了“教师天花板”。本研究提出无需强化学习的后见熵辅助学习框架，旨在弥合此类推理鸿沟。借鉴最近发展区教育理论，该框架协同整合三个核心模块：（1）引导式熵辅助修复机制，通过熵动态检测关键推理断点，并注入针对性后见提示以修复中断轨迹；（2）困惑度-不确定度比率评估器，采用严格过滤协议分离真实认知突破与虚假捷径；（3）渐进式答案引导课程演化策略，通过三阶段蒸馏流程组织从基础对齐到前沿突破的训练。在多基准测试上的广泛实验表明，该框架显著优于传统监督微调蒸馏方法及其他基线模型。

Abstract

Distilling reasoning capabilities from Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) into smaller models is typically constrained by the limitation of rejection sampling. Standard methods treat the teacher as a static filter, discarding complex "corner-case" problems where the teacher fails to explore valid solutions independently, thereby creating an artificial "Teacher Ceiling" for the student. In this work, we propose Hindsight Entropy-Assisted Learning (HEAL), an RL-free framework designed to bridge this reasoning gap. Drawing on the educational theory of the Zone of Proximal Development(ZPD), HEAL synergizes three core modules: (1) Guided Entropy-Assisted Repair (GEAR), an active intervention mechanism that detects critical reasoning breakpoints via entropy dynamics and injects targeted hindsight hints to repair broken trajectories; (2) Perplexity-Uncertainty Ratio Estimator (PURE), a rigorous filtering protocol that decouples genuine cognitive breakthroughs from spurious shortcuts; and (3) Progressive Answer-guided Curriculum Evolution (PACE), a three-stage distillation strategy that organizes training from foundational alignment to frontier breakthrough. Extensive experiments on multiple benchmarks demonstrate that HEAL significantly outperforms traditional SFT distillation and other baselines.

57. On The Complexity of Best-Arm Identification in Non-Stationary Linear Bandits FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Leo Maynard-Zhang, Zhihan Xiong, Kevin Jamieson, Maryam Fazel
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了非平稳线性赌博机中固定预算下的最优臂识别问题，提出了一个依赖于臂集的复杂度下界，并设计了匹配该下界的Adjacent-BAI算法。
摘要翻译

我们研究非平稳线性赌博机中的固定预算最优臂识别问题。具体而言，给定固定时间预算 $T\in \mathbb{N}$、有限臂集 $\mathcal{X} \subset \mathbb{R}^d$ 以及一个可能具有对抗性的未知参数序列 $\lbrace θ_t\rbrace_{t=1}^{T}$（即非平稳环境），学习者的目标是以高概率识别具有最大累积奖励的臂 $x_* = \arg\max_{x \in \mathcal{X}} x^\top\sum_{t=1}^T θ_t$。在此设定下，已知从 G-最优设计均匀采样臂会产生极小极大最优误差概率 $\exp\left(-Θ\left(T / H_{G}\right)\right)$，其中 $H_{G}$ 与维度 $d$ 成比例缩放。然而，这种复杂度度量过于悲观，因为它源自一个下界，该下界中的臂集仅由标准基向量构成，从而掩盖了具有更丰富几何结构的臂集可能带来的优势。为解决此问题，我们建立了一个依赖于臂集的下界，该下界对任意臂集均成立。受下界构建思想的启发，我们提出了邻接最优设计——这是著名的 $\mathcal{X}\mathcal{Y}$-最优设计的一种特化形式，并开发了 $\textsf{Adjacent-BAI}$ 算法。我们证明 $\textsf{Adjacent-BAI}$ 的误差概率在常数因子内匹配我们的下界，从而验证了下界的紧性，并确立了该设定下依赖于臂集的复杂度。

Abstract

We study the fixed-budget best-arm identification (BAI) problem in non-stationary linear bandits. Concretely, given a fixed time budget $T\in \mathbb{N}$, finite arm set $\mathcal{X} \subset \mathbb{R}^d$, and a potentially adversarial sequence of unknown parameters $\lbrace θ_t\rbrace_{t=1}^{T}$ (hence non-stationary), a learner aims to identify the arm with the largest cumulative reward $x_* = \arg\max_{x \in \mathcal{X}} x^\top\sum_{t=1}^T θ_t$ with high probability. In this setting, it is well-known that uniformly sampling arms from the G-optimal design yields a minimax-optimal error probability of $\exp\left(-Θ\left(T / H_{G}\right)\right)$, where $H_{G}$ scales proportionally with the dimension $d$. However, this notion of complexity is overly pessimistic, as it is derived from a lower bound in which the arm set consists only of the standard basis vectors, thus masking any potential advantages arising from arm sets with richer geometric structure. To address this, we establish an arm-set-dependent lower bound that, in contrast, holds for any arm set. Motivated by the ideas underlying our lower bound, we propose the Adjacent-optimal design, a specialization of the well-known $\mathcal{X}\mathcal{Y}$-optimal design, and develop the $\textsf{Adjacent-BAI}$ algorithm. We prove that the error probability of $\textsf{Adjacent-BAI}$ matches our lower bound up to constants, verifying the tightness of our lower bound, and establishing the arm-set-dependent complexity of this setting.

58. Federated Active Learning Under Extreme Non-IID and Global Class Imbalance FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Chen-Chen Zong, Sheng-Jun Huang
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了在极端非独立同分布和全局类别不平衡下联邦主动学习的性能下降问题，并提出了一种自适应的类别公平框架FairFAL，实验表明其在多个基准测试中优于现有方法。
摘要翻译

联邦主动学习（FAL）旨在隐私约束下降低标注成本，但在现实场景中，当面临严重的全局类别不平衡和高度异构的客户端时，其有效性会下降。我们对FAL中的查询模型选择进行了系统性研究，并揭示了一个核心发现：能够实现更均衡类别采样（尤其是对少数类）的模型，始终能带来更优的最终性能。此外，全局模型查询仅在全局分布高度不平衡且客户端数据相对同质时有益；否则，本地模型更为可取。基于这些发现，我们提出了FairFAL——一种自适应的类别公平FAL框架。FairFAL（1）通过轻量级预测差异推断全局不平衡性和本地-全局差异，从而自适应选择全局或本地查询模型；（2）利用全局特征进行原型引导的伪标注，以促进类别感知的查询；（3）采用两阶段不确定性-多样性平衡采样策略，并结合k中心优化。在五个基准数据集上的实验表明，在具有挑战性的长尾分布和非独立同分布（non-IID）设置下，FairFAL始终优于现有先进方法。代码发布于https://github.com/chenchenzong/FairFAL。

Abstract

Federated active learning (FAL) seeks to reduce annotation cost under privacy constraints, yet its effectiveness degrades in realistic settings with severe global class imbalance and highly heterogeneous clients. We conduct a systematic study of query-model selection in FAL and uncover a central insight: the model that achieves more class-balanced sampling, especially for minority classes, consistently leads to better final performance. Moreover, global-model querying is beneficial only when the global distribution is highly imbalanced and client data are relatively homogeneous; otherwise, the local model is preferable. Based on these findings, we propose FairFAL, an adaptive class-fair FAL framework. FairFAL (1) infers global imbalance and local-global divergence via lightweight prediction discrepancy, enabling adaptive selection between global and local query models; (2) performs prototype-guided pseudo-labeling using global features to promote class-aware querying; and (3) applies a two-stage uncertainty-diversity balanced sampling strategy with k-center refinement. Experiments on five benchmarks show that FairFAL consistently outperforms state-of-the-art approaches under challenging long-tailed and non-IID settings. The code is available at https://github.com/chenchenzong/FairFAL.

59. NasoVoce: A Nose-Mounted Low-Audibility Speech Interface for Always-Available Speech Interaction FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Jun Rekimoto, Yu Nishimura, Bojian Yang
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种鼻梁安装的低音量语音交互界面，通过融合麦克风和振动传感器信号，实现了在环境噪声中鲁棒的高质量语音识别，为持续可用的AI语音对话提供了实用解决方案。
摘要翻译

无声与耳语语音为实现与人工智能的持续可用语音交互提供了可能，但现有方法难以在词汇量、可穿戴性、静默性和抗噪鲁棒性之间取得平衡。我们提出了NasoVoce，一种集成麦克风与振动传感器的鼻梁佩戴式界面。该设备置于智能眼镜鼻托处，可无感地采集声学信号与振动信号。鼻梁位置靠近口部，能够获取骨传导与皮肤传导的语音信号，并可可靠捕获如耳语等低音量发声。麦克风虽能捕捉高质量音频，但对环境噪声极为敏感；反之，振动传感器虽具有强抗噪性，但信号质量较低。通过融合这两种互补的输入信号，NasoVoce能生成抗干扰的高质量语音。基于Whisper Large-v2模型、PESQ、STOI及MUSHRA评分的评估结果证实了其在识别率与语音质量上的提升。NasoVoce验证了实现持续可用、连续且隐蔽的人工智能语音会话实用界面的可行性。

Abstract

Silent and whispered speech offer promise for always-available voice interaction with AI, yet existing methods struggle to balance vocabulary size, wearability, silence, and noise robustness. We present NasoVoce, a nose-bridge-mounted interface that integrates a microphone and a vibration sensor. Positioned at the nasal pads of smart glasses, it unobtrusively captures both acoustic and vibration signals. The nasal bridge, close to the mouth, allows access to bone- and skin-conducted speech and enables reliable capture of low-volume utterances such as whispered speech. While the microphone captures high-quality audio, it is highly sensitive to environmental noise. Conversely, the vibration sensor is robust to noise but yields lower signal quality. By fusing these complementary inputs, NasoVoce generates high-quality speech robust against interference. Evaluation with Whisper Large-v2, PESQ, STOI, and MUSHRA ratings confirms improved recognition and quality. NasoVoce demonstrates the feasibility of a practical interface for always-available, continuous, and discreet AI voice conversations.

60. Data-Driven Integration Kernels for Interpretable Nonlocal Operator Learning FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Savannah L. Ferretti, Jerry Lin, Sara Shamekh, Jane W. Baldwin, Michael S. Pritchard, Tom Beucler
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文针对气候预测中非局部算子学习可解释性差的问题，提出了数据驱动的积分核框架，通过分离非局部信息聚合与局部非线性预测，在保持预测性能的同时大幅减少参数并提高模型可解释性，并在南亚季风降水预测中验证了其有效性。
摘要翻译

机器学习模型能够表征在水平空间、高度和时间维度上非局地的气候过程，通常通过以高度非线性的方式整合跨维度的信息来实现。虽然这可以提高预测技能，但随着非局地信息范围的扩大，习得的关系难以解释且容易过拟合。我们通过引入数据驱动的积分核框架来应对这一挑战，该框架通过明确将非局地信息聚合与局部非线性预测分离，为非局地算子学习添加结构。每个时空预测变量场首先使用可学习的核（定义为水平空间、高度和/或时间上的连续加权函数）进行积分，随后仅对生成的核积分特征及任何可选的局部输入施加局部非线性映射。这种设计将非线性相互作用限制在少量积分特征内，并使每个核可直接解释为一种加权模式，揭示哪些水平位置、垂直高度和过去时间步对预测贡献最大。我们以南亚季风降水为例，采用具有递增强化结构的神经网络模型层次（包括基线模型、非参数核模型和参数核模型）验证该框架。在整个模型层次中，基于核的模型以远少于可训练参数的数量实现了接近基线的性能，表明当施加适当的结构约束时，大部分相关非局地信息可通过少量可解释的积分操作捕获。

Abstract

Machine learning models can represent climate processes that are nonlocal in horizontal space, height, and time, often by combining information across these dimensions in highly nonlinear ways. While this can improve predictive skill, it makes learned relationships difficult to interpret and prone to overfitting as the extent of nonlocal information grows. We address this challenge by introducing data-driven integration kernels, a framework that adds structure to nonlocal operator learning by explicitly separating nonlocal information aggregation from local nonlinear prediction. Each spatiotemporal predictor field is first integrated using learnable kernels (defined as continuous weighting functions over horizontal space, height, and/or time), after which a local nonlinear mapping is applied only to the resulting kernel-integrated features and any optional local inputs. This design confines nonlinear interactions to a small set of integrated features and makes each kernel directly interpretable as a weighting pattern that reveals which horizontal locations, vertical levels, and past timesteps contribute most to the prediction. We demonstrate the framework for South Asian monsoon precipitation using a hierarchy of neural network models with increasing structure, including baseline, nonparametric kernel, and parametric kernel models. Across this hierarchy, kernel-based models achieve near-baseline performance with far fewer trainable parameters, showing that much of the relevant nonlocal information can be captured through a small set of interpretable integrations when appropriate structural constraints are imposed.

61. How to make the most of your masked language model for protein engineering FAIL

Authors: Calvin McCarter, Nick Bhattacharya, Sebastian W. Ober, Hunter Elliott
Published: 2026-03-11

摘要翻译

近年来，大量蛋白质语言模型相继发布。然而，关于如何从中进行最佳采样以优化目标生物学特性的研究相对较少。我们通过提出一种针对掩码语言模型（MLMs）的灵活高效采样方法，并结合实际抗体治疗项目在计算机模拟和体外实验中系统评估模型与方法，填补了这一空白。首先，我们提出基于随机束搜索的采样方法，该方法利用了MLMs在评估序列单点编辑邻域整体伪困惑度方面的高效性。将生成问题重新定义为全序列评估，使得多目标优化引导具备灵活性。其次，我们报告了在抗体工程场景下开展的广泛体外对照评估结果。研究表明，采样方法的选择对结果的影响至少与模型选择同等重要，这为这一尚未充分探索领域的未来研究提供了动力。

Abstract

A plethora of protein language models have been released in recent years. Yet comparatively little work has addressed how to best sample from them to optimize desired biological properties. We fill this gap by proposing a flexible, effective sampling method for masked language models (MLMs), and by systematically evaluating models and methods both in silico and in vitro on actual antibody therapeutics campaigns. Firstly, we propose sampling with stochastic beam search, exploiting the fact that MLMs are remarkably efficient at evaluating the pseudo-perplexity of the entire 1-edit neighborhood of a sequence. Reframing generation in terms of entire-sequence evaluation enables flexible guidance with multiple optimization objectives. Secondly, we report results from our extensive in vitro head-to-head evaluation for the antibody engineering setting. This reveals that choice of sampling method is at least as impactful as the model used, motivating future research into this under-explored area.

62. What do near-optimal learning rate schedules look like? FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Hiroki Naganuma, Atish Agarwala, Priya Kasimbeg, George E. Dahl
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了神经网络训练中最佳学习率调度形状的问题，通过设计搜索程序在参数化调度族中寻找最优形状，发现预热和衰减是良好调度的稳健特征，并证明常用调度族在这些任务上并非最优。
摘要翻译

神经网络训练中一个尚未解决的基本问题是：对于给定任务，最佳学习率调度曲线应是何种形态？学习率调度的选择是训练成败的关键因素，但除了需要某种形式的热身阶段和衰减机制外，学界对于优秀调度曲线的构成尚未达成共识。为解答此问题，我们设计了一种搜索程序，用于在参数化的调度曲线族中寻找最优形态。我们的方法将调度曲线形态与基础学习率分离，从而避免了基础学习率在跨调度比较中成为主导因素。我们将该搜索程序应用于三类任务中的多种调度曲线族：线性回归、CIFAR-10图像分类以及Wikitext103小规模语言建模。实验表明，我们的搜索程序确实能普遍找到接近最优的调度方案。研究发现，热身阶段和衰减机制是优秀调度方案中具有鲁棒性的特征，而常用调度曲线族在这些任务中并非最优。最后，我们探究了调度形态搜索的输出如何受其他优化超参数的影响，发现权重衰减（weight decay）对最优调度形态可能产生显著影响。据我们所知，本研究结果代表了迄今为止关于深度神经网络训练中接近最优调度曲线形态的最全面研究成果。

Abstract

A basic unanswered question in neural network training is: what is the best learning rate schedule shape for a given workload? The choice of learning rate schedule is a key factor in the success or failure of the training process, but beyond having some kind of warmup and decay, there is no consensus on what makes a good schedule shape. To answer this question, we designed a search procedure to find the best shapes within a parameterized schedule family. Our approach factors out the schedule shape from the base learning rate, which otherwise would dominate cross-schedule comparisons. We applied our search procedure to a variety of schedule families on three workloads: linear regression, image classification on CIFAR-10, and small-scale language modeling on Wikitext103. We showed that our search procedure indeed generally found near-optimal schedules. We found that warmup and decay are robust features of good schedules, and that commonly used schedule families are not optimal on these workloads. Finally, we explored how the outputs of our shape search depend on other optimization hyperparameters, and found that weight decay can have a strong effect on the optimal schedule shape. To the best of our knowledge, our results represent the most comprehensive results on near-optimal schedule shapes for deep neural network training, to date.

63. Regime-aware financial volatility forecasting via in-context learning FAIL

Authors: Saba Asaad, Shayan Mohajer Hamidi, Ali Bereyhi

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于大语言模型的机制感知上下文学习框架，用于非平稳市场条件下的金融波动率预测，实验表明该方法在多个金融数据集上优于传统波动率预测方法和直接单样本学习，尤其是在高波动时期。
摘要翻译

本研究提出一种基于市场状态感知的上下文学习框架，利用大语言模型在非平稳市场条件下进行金融波动率预测。该框架部署预训练大语言模型，使其能够在不进行参数微调的情况下，基于历史波动模式进行推理并调整预测结果。我们开发了一种基于理想预测器的优化流程，从训练数据中构建具有市场状态感知能力的演示样本。随后，大语言模型作为上下文学习器，根据输入序列并采用基于估计市场状态标签的条件采样演示，预测下一阶段波动率。这种条件采样策略使大语言模型仅通过上下文推理，即可使其预测适应不同市场状态下的波动动态。在多个金融数据集上的实验表明，所提出的市场状态感知上下文学习框架在预测性能上优于传统波动率预测方法和直接单样本学习方法，尤其在市场高波动时期表现更为突出。

Abstract

This work introduces a regime-aware in-context learning framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) for financial volatility forecasting under nonstationary market conditions. The proposed approach deploys pretrained LLMs to reason over historical volatility patterns and adjust their predictions without parameter fine-tuning. We develop an oracle-guided refinement procedure that constructs regime-aware demonstrations from training data. An LLM is then deployed as an in-context learner that predicts the next-step volatility from the input sequence using demonstrations sampled conditional to the estimated market label. This conditional sampling strategy enables the LLM to adapt its predictions to regime-dependent volatility dynamics through contextual reasoning alone. Experiments with multiple financial datasets show that the proposed regime-aware in-context learning framework outperforms both classical volatility forecasting approaches and direct one-shot learning, especially during high-volatility periods.

摘要翻译

大型语言模型（LLMs）的迅速崛起及其捕捉语义关系的能力，使其被广泛应用于众多领域。文本属性图（Text-attributed Graphs, TAGs）是一个典型示例，其中LLMs可与图神经网络结合以提升节点分类性能。在TAGs中，每个节点都与文本内容相关联，此类图常见于社交网络、引文图、推荐系统等多个领域。从TAGs中有效学习，能够更好地融合图的结构与文本表征，从而提升相关领域的决策质量。本文提出GaLoRA，一种参数高效的框架，将结构信息整合到LLMs中。GaLoRA在TAGs的节点分类任务中展现出竞争力，其性能与最先进模型相当，而所需参数量仅占完整LLM微调参数的0.24%。我们在三个真实世界数据集上进行实验，验证了GaLoRA在TAGs上有效融合结构与语义信息的能力。

Abstract

The rapid rise of large language models (LLMs) and their ability to capture semantic relationships has led to their adoption in a wide range of applications. Text-attributed graphs (TAGs) are a notable example where LLMs can be combined with Graph Neural Networks to improve the performance of node classification. In TAGs, each node is associated with textual content and such graphs are commonly seen in various domains such as social networks, citation graphs, recommendation systems, etc. Effectively learning from TAGs would enable better representations of both structural and textual representations of the graph and improve decision-making in relevant domains. We present GaLoRA, a parameter-efficient framework that integrates structural information into LLMs. GaLoRA demonstrates competitive performance on node classification tasks with TAGs, performing on par with state-of-the-art models with just 0.24% of the parameter count required by full LLM fine-tuning. We experiment with three real-world datasets to showcase GaLoRA's effectiveness in combining structural and semantical information on TAGs.

Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文提出并分析了一种在光学晶格中实现Emery模型的量子模拟方案，用于研究铜酸盐和无限层镍酸盐的高温超导物理，为理解非常规超导体提供了新途径。
摘要翻译

铜氧化物高温超导的微观起源依然是凝聚态物理领域的核心未解问题之一。越来越多的实验与理论证据表明，裸单带费米-哈伯德模型可能无法完全涵盖铜氧化物的超导等特性，这促使我们重新审视铜氧平面的经典三带模型——埃默里模型，单带模型最初正是由此推导而来。本文提出并分析了一种量子模拟方案，旨在利用当前超冷原子量子模拟平台，在与铜氧化物及无限层镍酸盐相关的参数区间内实现埃默里模型，从而能够在当前数值方法难以处理的系统尺度上探索三带物理。具体而言，我们证明可通过设计一种叠加排斥势图案的二维光晶格，来研究与铜氧化物及无限层镍酸盐相关的埃默里模型可变参数区间内的低温特性。我们的研究结果为利用超冷原子量子模拟器实现真实材料模拟、深入理解非常规超导体的物理机制开辟了道路。

Abstract

The microscopic origin of high-temperature superconductivity in cuprates remains one of the central open questions in condensed matter physics. Growing experimental and theoretical evidence suggests that the bare single-band Fermi-Hubbard model may not fully capture properties of cuprates such as superconductivity, motivating us to revisit the canonical three-band model of the copper-oxide planes - the Emery model - from which the single-band counterpart was originally derived. Here, we propose and analyze a quantum simulation scheme for realizing the Emery model in regimes relevant to cuprates and infinite-layer nickelates with today's ultracold atom quantum simulation platforms, enabling the exploration of the three-band physics on system sizes that are challenging for current numerical methods. Specifically, we show that a two-dimensional optical lattice with a superimposed pattern of repulsive potentials can be designed to study low-temperature properties for variable parameter regimes of the Emery model relevant to cuprates as well as infinite-layer nickelates. Our results pave the way for real material simulations with ultracold atom quantum simulators and a better understanding of the physics of unconventional superconductors.

66. Quantum-to-classical correspondence in Krylov complexity FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Gastón F. Scialchi, Augusto J. Roncaglia, Diego A. Wisniacki
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子Krylov复杂度在经典极限下的对应关系，证明了在适当定义下经典Krylov空间可作为量子Krylov空间的渐近展开，并通过示例分析了Krylov复杂度演化与相空间表示的关系。
摘要翻译

我们研究了具有经典极限的幺正映射驱动演化过程中Krylov空间的量子-经典对应性。这需要明确定义相应的量子与经典算符、内积及初始态。我们证明，基于这些定义，纯经典Krylov空间确实可通过量子Krylov空间在$\hbar\to 0$渐近展开获得，并提供了若干此类对应的实例。借助这些实例，我们分析了Krylov复杂度演化中与Krylov态相空间表示相关的一般特性。此外，我们探讨了实现对应的其他定义方式及其失败原因。本文通过Krylov视角理解幺正演化的复杂度与遍历性及其与经典动力学概念的联系，迈出了第一步。

Abstract

We study quantum-to-classical correspondence of the Krylov space for evolutions driven by unitary maps with a classical limit. This entails a proper definition of corresponding quantum and classical operators, inner products and initial states. We prove that with these definitions the purely classical Krylov space is indeed obtained as the asymptotic $\hbar\to 0$ expansion of the quantum Krylov space, and provide several examples of such correspondence. We use these examples to analyze some general aspects about the evolution of the Krylov complexity as they relate to the phase-space representation for the Krylov states. Additionally, we discuss alternative definitions to obtain the correspondence and why they fail. This paper constitutes a first step in understanding complexity and ergodicity of unitary evolution through the Krylov perspective as they relate to classical dynamical notions.

67. Mitigating crosstalk errors for simultaneous single-qubit gates on a superconducting quantum processor FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Jaap J. Wesdorp, Eric Hyyppä, Joona Andersson, Janos Adam, Rohit Beriwal, Ville Bergholm, Saga Dahl, Simone Diego Fasciati, Alejandro Gomez Friero, Zheming Gao, Daria Gusenkova, Andrew Guthrie, Johannes Heinsoo, Tuukka Hiltunen, Keiran Holland, Amin Hosseinkhani, Sinan Inel, Joni Ikonen, Shan W. Jolin, Kristinn Juliusson, Seung-Goo Kim, Anton Komlev, Roope Kokkoniemi, Otto Koskinen, Joonas Kylmälä, Alessandro Landra, Julia Lamprich, Magdalena Lehmuskoski, Nizar Lethif, Per Liebermann, Tianyi Li, Aleksi Lintunen, Fabian Marxer, Kunal Mitra, Jakub Mrożek, Lucas Ortega, Miha Papič, Matti Partanen, Alexander Plyushch, Stefan Pogorzalek, Michael Renger, Jussi Ritvas, Sampo Saarinen, Indrajeet Sagar, Matthew Sarsby, Mykhailo Savytskyi, Ville Selinmaa, Ivan Takmakov, Brian Tarasinski, Francesca Tosto, David Vasey, Panu Vesanen, Jeroen Verjauw, Alpo Välimaa, Nicola Wurz, Hsiang-Sheng Ku, Frank Deppe, Juha Hassel, Caspar Ockeloen-Korppi, Wei Liu, Jani Tuorila, Chun Fai Chan, Attila Geresdi, Antti Vepsäläinen
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该研究通过结合基于模型的量子比特频率优化和脉冲整形技术，在49量子比特超导量子处理器上实现了同时单量子比特门的串扰误差缓解，将平均同时门保真度提升至99.96%，并减少了并行操作所需的量子比特频率带宽。
摘要翻译

在超导量子处理器中，单量子比特门通常通过专用控制线施加微波脉冲来实现。然而，由于电容耦合以及跃迁频率紧密相邻的系统中波函数重叠所引起的串扰，这些微波脉冲也可能驱动其他量子比特。相对于孤立门操作，串扰和频率拥挤会加剧并行单量子比特操作中的错误，从而成为超导量子处理器规模扩展的主要瓶颈。本研究结合基于模型的量子比特频率优化与脉冲整形技术，在一台49量子比特的超导量子处理器上展示了单量子比特门中的串扰误差抑制。我们提出并通过实验验证了一种解析模型，该模型描述了由微波串扰引起的并行单量子比特门误差，其误差大小取决于给定的脉冲形状。通过采用基于模型的量子比特频率优化策略，我们最小化了整个处理器中由串扰引起的误差，并在16纳秒的门操作时长下实现了平均并行单量子比特门保真度达99.96%，接近平均独立门保真度。为了进一步降低高串扰量子比特对上的并行误差及所需量子比特频率带宽，我们引入了一种串扰跃迁抑制（CTS, crosstalk transition suppression）脉冲整形技术，该技术能最小化导致泄漏和串扰误差的跃迁附近的频谱能量。最后，我们将CTS与全器件范围的基于模型的频率优化相结合，并通过实验证明了高保真度并行门操作所需量子比特频率带宽的系统性降低，这一结果得到了对多达1000量子比特系统的仿真支持。通过缓解并行单量子比特操作对量子比特频率带宽的限制，本工作为向更大规模量子处理器扩展迈出了重要一步。

Abstract

Single-qubit gates on superconducting quantum processors are typically implemented using microwave pulses applied through dedicated control lines. However, these microwave pulses may also drive other qubits due to crosstalk arising from capacitive coupling and wavefunction overlap in systems with closely spaced transition frequencies. Crosstalk and frequency crowding increase errors during simultaneous single-qubit operations relative to isolated gates, thus forming a major bottleneck for scaling superconducting quantum processors. In this work, we combine model-based qubit frequency optimization with pulse shaping to demonstrate crosstalk error mitigation in single-qubit gates on a 49-qubit superconducting quantum processor. We introduce and experimentally verify an analytical model of simultaneous single-qubit gate error caused by microwave crosstalk that depends on a given pulse shape. By employing a model-based optimization strategy of qubit frequencies, we minimize the crosstalk-induced error across the processor and achieve a mean simultaneous single-qubit gate fidelity of 99.96% for a 16-ns gate duration, approaching the mean individual gate fidelity. To further reduce the simultaneous error and required qubit frequency bandwidth on high-crosstalk qubit pairs, we introduce a crosstalk transition suppression (CTS) pulse shaping technique that minimizes the spectral energy around transitions inducing leakage and crosstalk errors. Finally, we combine CTS with model-based frequency optimization across the device and experimentally show a systematic reduction in the required qubit frequency bandwidth for high-fidelity simultaneous gates, supported by simulations of systems with up to 1000 qubits. By alleviating constraints on qubit frequency bandwidth for parallel single-qubit operations, this work represents an important step for scaling towards larger quantum processors.

68. Universality of Classically Trainable, Quantum-Deployed Boson-Sampling Generative Models FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Andrii Kurkin, Ulysse Chabaud, Zoltán Kolarovszki, Bence Bakó, Zoltán Zimborás, Vedran Dunjko
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了玻色采样生成模型（BSBM）的经典可训练性和量子部署的普适性，证明了通过扩展模型可以实现普适生成能力，同时保持经典训练的效率和量子采样的计算困难性。
摘要翻译

近期关于瞬时量子多项式时间（IQP）量子电路玻恩机（QCBM）的研究揭示了一种极具前景的生成建模范式：经典训练，量子部署。在此框架下，训练目标可在经典计算机上高效评估，而从训练所得模型中采样仍可能具有经典计算上的难解性。此外，在IQP-QCBM框架中，已证明通过引入辅助量子比特扩展模型族可实现通用性。本文探讨线性光学生成模型是否具有类似性质。为此，我们提出了玻色采样玻恩机（BSBM）。我们的分析沿用了IQP-QCBM的研究路径并加以调整。借助近期可实现线性光学中广泛期望值经典近似的研究成果，我们证明BSBM可在多种损失函数族下进行经典训练。接着，我们论证“基础”BSBM并非通用生成模型，而通过扩展模型可在保持高效经典训练与采样难解性的同时实现通用性。在我们的方法中，我们引入并分析了常数函数后处理的作用，推广了IQP-QCBM的构建方案——该方案在适当条件下可在保持模型经典模拟难解性的同时实现通用性。我们展示了一类由单一超参数定义的BSBM族，其表达能力可单调增强至通用性，同时仍能表征显见的难解分布。此外，我们讨论了在损失函数梯度可高效估计的意义上实现高效经典训练的可能模式。

Abstract

Recent work on the instantaneous quantum polynomial-time (IQP) quantum-circuit Born machine (QCBM) highlights a promising paradigm for generative modeling: train classically, deploy quantumly. In this setting, the training objective can be evaluated efficiently on a classical computer, while sampling from the resulting model may still be classically intractable. Furthermore, in the IQP-QCBM framework, extending the model family with ancillary qubits has been proven to yield universality. This paper asks whether similar results hold for linear-optical generative models. To this end, we introduce the Boson Sampling Born Machine (BSBM). Our analysis retraces analogous steps as were found for IQP-QCBMs with twists. Using recent results that enable classical approximation of broad classes of expectation values in linear optics, we show that BSBMs can be trained classically for wide families of loss functions. Next, we argue that "basic" BSBMs are not universal generative models, and that universality can be achieved by expanding the model while preserving efficient classical training and sampling hardness. In our approach, we introduce and analyze the role of constant-function postprocessing, generalizing the construction for IQP-QCBMs, which under suitable conditions can lead to universality while preserving the hardness of classically simulating the models. We showcase a family of BSBMs, characterized by a single hyperparameter, that allows for a monotonic increase in expressivity toward universality while retaining the capacity to represent ostensibly hard distributions. Furthermore, we discuss the possible modalities for the efficient classical training, in the sense of efficient estimation of gradients of the loss function.

69. Permutation-invariant codes: a numerical study and qudit constructions FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Liam J. Bond, Jiří Minář, Māris Ozols, Arghavan Safavi-Naini, Vladyslav Visnevskyi
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文研究了置换不变量子纠错码的数值特性和构造方法，主要发现包括提出了关于比特码块长度下界的猜想、展示了增加物理维度可接近量子Singleton界、以及将比特构造方法扩展到量子比特的半解析扩展。
摘要翻译

我们研究了置换不变（Permutation-Invariant, PI）量子纠错码，该码利用维度为 $\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{P}$ 的物理量子比特（qudit），在 PI 态中编码一个维度为 $\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{L}$ 的逻辑量子比特。我们将适用于 $d-1$ 个删除错误的 Knill–Laflamme (KL) 条件从量子比特（qubit）推广到量子比特，并数值研究了量子比特（$\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{L} = \mathrm{d}_\mathrm{P} = 2$）和量子比特（$\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{L} > 2$ 或 $\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{P} > 2$）的 PI 码。我们分析了码块长度 $n$ 随码距 $d$ 变化的标度关系，并与 Ouyang、Aydin–Alekseyev–Barg (AAB) 以及 Pollatsek–Ruskai (PR) 提出的现有 PI 码族进行了比较。我们的三个主要发现是：（i）我们推测，能够纠正最多 $d-1$ 个删除错误的量子比特 PI 码，其块长度满足 $n(d) \geq (3d^2 + 1) / 4$，这意味着其码距存在上界 $d \leq \sqrt{12n-3}/3$，并且 PR 码可以达到此上界。（ii）对于编码单个量子比特的量子比特 PI 码，我们数值观察到，增加物理维度 $\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{P}$ 会导致 $n$ 单调递减并趋近于量子 Singleton 界 $n(d) \geq 2d-1$。（iii）我们提出了一种将量子比特 AAB 构造半解析地推广到量子比特的方法，该方法通过求解线性规划来获得显式解。因此，我们的结果为量子比特和量子比特 PI 码的块长度标度下界提供了关键见解，并展示了在 PI 码背景下增加物理局域维度的优势。

Abstract

We investigate Permutation-Invariant (PI) quantum error-correcting codes encoding a logical qudit of dimension $\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{L}$ in PI states using physical qudits of dimension $\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{P}$. We extend the Knill--Laflamme (KL) conditions for $d-1$ deletion errors from qubits to qudits and investigate numerically both qubit ($\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{L} = \mathrm{d}_\mathrm{P} = 2$) and qudit ($\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{L} > 2$ or $\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{P} > 2$) PI codes. We analyze the scaling of the block length $n$ in terms of the code distance $d$, and compare to existing families of PI codes due to Ouyang, Aydin--Alekseyev--Barg (AAB) and Pollatsek--Ruskai (PR). Our three main findings are: (i) We conjecture that qubit PI codes correcting up to $d-1$ deletion errors have block length $n(d) \geq (3d^2 + 1) / 4$, which implies an upper bound $d \leq \sqrt{12n-3}/3$ on their code distance, and that PR codes can saturate this bound. (ii) For qudit PI codes encoding a single qudit we numerically observe that increasing $\mathrm{d}_\mathrm{P}$ results in $n$ monotonically decreasing and approaching the quantum Singleton bound $n(d) \geq 2d-1$. (iii) We propose a semi-analytic extension of the qubit AAB construction to qudits that finds explicit solutions by solving a linear program. Our results therefore provide key insights into lower bounds on the block length scaling of both qubit and qudit PI codes, and demonstrate the benefit of increased physical local dimension in the context of PI codes.

70. Violating the All-or-Nothing Picture of Local Charges in Non-Hermitian Bosonic Chains FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Mizuki Yamaguchi, Naoto Shiraishi
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文通过构造非厄米玻色子链中的反例，证明了局域电荷并不总是表现出全有或全无行为，并给出了这类系统中k-局域电荷存在的充要条件，从而对可积性进行了分类并发现了新的可积模型。
摘要翻译

我们针对“局域可对易电荷呈现全有或全无行为”这一普遍经验预期提出了明确反例。在具有对称最近邻跃迁及任意在位项（包括非厄米项）的玻色子链体系中，我们展示了存在仅对特定k值具备k-局域电荷而非所有k值的系统。具体而言，我们构建了具有3-局域电荷但不存在其他非平凡局域电荷的非厄米模型，以及具备除k=4外所有k值局域电荷的模型。这些结果表明，基于3-局域电荷的Grabowski-Mathieu可积性检验并不具有普适性。我们进一步给出了此类体系中k-局域电荷存在的充要条件，从而实现了完备分类并发现了新的可积模型。

Abstract

We present explicit counterexamples to a widespread empirical expectation that local commuting charges display all-or-nothing behavior. In the class of bosonic chains with symmetric nearest-neighbor hopping and arbitrary on-site terms (including non-Hermitian terms), we exhibit systems that possess k-local charges for some but not all k. Concretely, we construct non-Hermitian models with a 3-local charge but no other nontrivial local charges and models with k-local charges for all k except k = 4. These results show that the Grabowski--Mathieu integrability test based on 3-local charges is not universally applicable. We further give necessary and sufficient conditions for the existence of k-local charges in this class, yielding an exhaustive classification and uncovering additional integrable models.

71. Generalized Reduced-Density-Matrix Quantum Monte Carlo Gives Access to More FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Zhiyan Wang, Zhe Wang, Bin-Bin Mao, Zheng Yan
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于广义约化密度矩阵的量子蒙特卡罗新框架，解决了传统方法中难以测量非对角算符和动态可观测量的问题，从而实现了更丰富的量子系统信息提取。
摘要翻译

在量子蒙特卡罗（QMC）方法中，能够高效测量的内容很大程度上取决于所采样的对象。当采样对象为配分函数时，一大类可观测量（包括一般的非对角算符）通常无法作为直接估计量获得。本文通过引入一个范式转变：将模拟对象从配分函数替换为广义约化密度矩阵（generalized reduced density matrix, GRDM）。这一重构从根源上消除了测量瓶颈，并将约化描述在维度缩减上的优势从静态量扩展至动力学可观测量，从而实现了更丰富的信息提取。作为实质性验证，该框架使得定向循环算法能够同时测量等时与非对角虚时可观测量，后者可直接用于获取动力学谱。该框架还能测量用于诊断混合态中强对称性破缺至弱对称性破缺的Rényi-1关联子。本工作为QMC内的全息表征建立了一个统一框架。

Abstract

In quantum Monte Carlo (QMC), what can be measured efficiently is largely determined by what is sampled. When the sampled object is the partition function, a broad class of observables, including general off-diagonal operators, is typically unavailable as direct estimators. In this article, we introduce a paradigm shift by replacing the partition function with a generalized reduced density matrix (GRDM) as the simulated object. This reformulation removes the measurement bottleneck at its source and extends the dimensional-reduction advantage of reduced descriptions from static quantities to dynamical observables, thereby enabling much richer information extraction. As substantial demonstrations, the framework allows the directed-loop algorithm to measure both equal-time and imaginary-time off-diagonal observables, with the latter giving direct access to dynamical spectra. It also enables measurements of Rényi-1 correlators that diagnose strong-to-weak symmetry breaking in mixed states. This work establishes a unified framework for holographic characterization within QMC.

72. Efficient construction of $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge-invariant bases for the Quantum Minimally Entangled Typical Thermal States algorithm FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Reita Maeno
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文解决了在有限温度和有限密度下量子规范场论计算中保持规范不变性的挑战，提出了一种用于Z2规范约束系统的高效量子最小纠缠典型热态算法，并通过数值模拟验证了其在(1+1)维Z2规范理论中的正确性。
摘要翻译

在有限温度与有限密度下规范理论的量子计算中，对热系综所有贡献态强制执行高斯定律是一项挑战。尽管已有多种实现规范约束的技术被提出，但它们往往涉及实际权衡。在本工作中，我们采用量子最小纠缠典型热态（QMETTS）算法处理 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 规范约束系统，该方法使我们能够在平衡这些权衡的同时，捕捉包含化学势的热平衡态。为确保规范不变性在整个计算过程中得以保持，同时维持计算效率，我们在算法内推导了具体的测量基。此外，由于量子硬件上期望值的估计本质上是含噪声的，我们严格考虑了估计期望值时的散粒噪声，并提出了一种比先前工作更高效的采样方法。我们通过数值研究一个耦合交错费米子的（1+1）维 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 规范理论，验证了所提方法的有效性。我们提出的算法在有限温度与有限密度下准确重现了正确的平衡态。

Abstract

In quantum computations of gauge theories at finite temperature and finite density, it is challenging to enforce Gauss's law for all states contributing to the thermal ensemble. While various techniques for implementing gauge constraints have been proposed, they often involve practical trade-offs. In this work, we adopt the Quantum Minimally Entangled Typical Thermal States (QMETTS) algorithm for $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge-constrained systems, which allows us to capture thermal equilibrium states with chemical potential while mitigating these trade-offs. To ensure that gauge invariance is preserved throughout the procedure while maintaining computational efficiency, we derive the specific measurement bases within the algorithm. Furthermore, since the estimation of expectation values on quantum hardware is inherently noisy, we rigorously account for shot noise in estimating expectation values, and propose a sampling method that is more efficient than those in previous works. We validate our approach numerically by studying a (1+1)-dimensional $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge theory coupled to staggered fermions. Our proposed algorithm reproduces the correct equilibrium states at finite temperature and finite density.

73. Variational Adaptive Gaussian Decomposition: Scalable Quadrature-Free Time-Sliced Thawed Gaussian Dynamics FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Rahul Sharma, Amartya Bose
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种变分自适应高斯分解方法，用于量子动力学中的时间切片半经典传播，通过神经网络优化高斯波包参数，实现了可扩展的量子动力学模拟。
摘要翻译

时间切片已成为将半经典传播纳入实时路径积分表述并恢复完整量子力学动力学的一种策略。其核心步骤是将时间演化的波函数分解为高斯波包叠加态。本文提出了一种无需数值积分的变分框架用于高斯波包分解，将其重新表述为一个优化问题：通过选择高斯波包的参数，使其与时间演化波函数的重叠度最大化。该优化过程采用自编码器-解码器神经网络实现，其表示形式在传播过程中进行自适应重优化。分解中的每个波包代表了底层半经典流形的一个局域化片段，同时保留了所有自由度之间的完全关联性。这种变分自适应高斯分解（Variational Adaptive Gaussian Decomposition, VAGD）方法能够产生紧凑的高斯展开，为时间切片半经典量子动力学提供了一条可扩展的路径。该方法具有普适性，将其应用于促进解冻高斯近似（Thawed Gaussian Approximation, TGA）模拟的时间切片，能够为系统性地将半经典结果提升至完整量子力学结果提供一条可行途径。

Abstract

Time-slicing has emerged as a strategy for incorporating semiclassical propagation into real-time path integral formulation and recovering full quantum mechanical dynamics. A central step is the decomposition of a time-evolved wave function into a superposition of Gaussian wave packets. Here we introduce a quadrature-free variational framework for Gaussian wave packet decomposition, reformulating it as an optimization problem in which the parameters of Gaussian wave packets are chosen to maximize the overlap with the time-evolving wave function. An autoencoder-decoder neural network is used for this optimization, with the representation being adaptively reoptimized during propagation. Each wave packet in this decomposition represents a localized patch of the underlying semiclassical manifold, while retaining full correlations between all degrees of freedom. This variational adaptive Gaussian decomposition (VAGD) approach yields a compact Gaussian expansion, providing a scalable route to time-sliced semiclassical quantum dynamics. While general, applying VAGD to facilitate time-slicing of thawed Gaussian approximation (TGA) simulation allows a route to improving the semiclassical result to the full quantum mechanical result in a systematic manner.

74. Supercurrents in Josephson junctions with chiral molecular potentials FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Oleg Kuliashov, Alberto Cappellaro, Oded Millo, Yossi Paltiel, Mikhail Lemeshko, Ragheed Alhyder
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该研究通过理论建模发现手性分子功能化的约瑟夫森结中，自旋超流对手性分子结构表现出显著依赖性和各向异性响应，而电荷超流则基本不受影响，从而为利用超导自旋输运检测分子手性提供了新平台。
摘要翻译

本文研究了手性分子势对超导约瑟夫森结中相位相干输运的影响。在Bogoliubov-de Gennes紧束缚框架下，我们模拟了通过吸附手性分子功能化的SNS（超导体-正常金属-超导体）结，其中分子产生的静电梯度在正常区域诱导出自旋轨道耦合。研究发现，在对称、零磁场构型中，平衡电荷电流-相位关系对手性分子构型基本不敏感。相比之下，自旋超电流表现出显著的手性依赖响应，相反的对映异构体会产生截然不同且各向异性的自旋极化约瑟夫森电流。由此产生的手性对比度可通过分子取向和诱导自旋轨道耦合强度等控制参数进行增强。这些电流的温度依赖性进一步表明，在远低于超导临界温度的温度范围内，手性依赖特征持续存在。这些结果确立了约瑟夫森干涉测量法作为一种相位敏感且易于操作的平台，可用于检测分子手性，并突显了自旋极化超导输运作为将手性分子功能集成到超导自旋电子器件中的一条前景广阔的路径。

Abstract

The influence of chiral molecular potentials on phase-coherent transport in superconducting Josephson junctions is investigated. Within a Bogoliubov-de Gennes tight-binding framework, an SNS junction functionalized by adsorbed chiral molecules is modeled, where electrostatic gradients generated by the molecules induce spin-orbit coupling in the normal region. The equilibrium charge current-phase relation is found to remain largely insensitive to molecular chirality in symmetric, zero-field configurations. In contrast, the spin supercurrent exhibits a pronounced chirality-dependent response, with opposite enantiomers producing distinct and anisotropic spin-polarized Josephson currents. The resulting handedness contrast can be enhanced through control parameters such as molecular orientation and the strength of the induced spin-orbit coupling. The temperature dependence of these currents further shows that the chirality-dependent signatures persist across a range of temperatures well below the superconducting critical temperature. These results establish Josephson interferometry as a phase-sensitive and accessible platform for detecting molecular chirality and highlight spin-polarized superconducting transport as a promising route toward integrating chiral molecular functionality into superconducting spintronic devices.

75. Hybridlane: A Software Development Kit for Hybrid Continuous-Discrete Variable Quantum Computing FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Jim Furches, Timothy J. Stavenger, Carlos Ortiz Marrero
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文针对混合连续-离散变量量子计算缺乏统一软件框架的问题，开发了Hybridlane SDK，实现了自动线路类型推断、低内存消耗的电路描述以及多后端支持，提升了混合量子系统的编程效率和可扩展性。
摘要翻译

混合量子计算系统通过将离散变量量子比特与连续变量量子模相结合，为量子模拟、纠错和传感应用提供了显著优势。然而，现有的量子软件框架缺乏对混合电路表达与操作的原生支持，迫使开发者使用碎片化的工具链或依赖与模拟耦合的表示方法，从而限制了可扩展性。本文提出Hybridlane——一个开源的软件开发工具包，为混合连续-离散变量量子计算提供统一的前端。Hybridlane引入了自动线路类型推断功能，无需手动标注即可区分量子比特与量子模，实现了电路正确性的编译时验证。通过将门语义与矩阵表示解耦，Hybridlane能够以最小内存消耗描述宽而深的电路，且无需依赖模拟。该框架遵循成熟的指令集架构，实现了完整的混合量子门及分解算法库，同时保持与PennyLane庞大量子比特算法库的兼容性。此外，它支持包括基于Bosonic Qiskit的经典模拟和面向桑迪亚国家实验室QSCOUT离子阱的硬件编译在内的多种后端。我们通过玻色量子相位估计和离子阱校准工作流展示了Hybridlane的核心能力。

Abstract

Hybrid quantum computing systems that combine discrete-variable qubits with continuous-variable qumodes offer promising advantages for quantum simulation, error correction, and sensing applications. However, existing quantum software frameworks lack native support for expressing and manipulating hybrid circuits, forcing developers to work with fragmented toolchains or rely on simulation-coupled representations that limit scalability. We present Hybridlane, an open-source software development kit providing a unified frontend for hybrid continuous-discrete variable quantum computing. Hybridlane introduces automatic wire type inference to distinguish qubits from qumodes without manual annotations, enabling compile-time validation of circuit correctness. By decoupling gate semantics from matrix representations, Hybridlane can describe wide and deep circuits with minimal memory consumption and without requiring simulation. The framework implements a comprehensive library of hybrid gates and decompositions following established instruction set architectures, while remaining compatible with PennyLane's extensive qubit algorithm library. Furthermore, it supports multiple backends including classical simulation with Bosonic Qiskit and hardware compilation to Sandia National Laboratories' QSCOUT ion trap. We demonstrate Hybridlane's capabilities through bosonic quantum phase estimation and ion trap calibration workflows.

摘要翻译

量子超图态通过引入超边描述多量子比特相互作用，从而扩展了已被深入研究的图态范畴。它们为表征具有真多体纠缠的量子态族提供了一个强有力的理论框架。本综述对超图态在量子信息理论中的形式结构、纠缠特性与操作相关性进行了简明概述。我们首先介绍其数学基础以及稳定子形式体系的推广。重点聚焦于其纠缠性质，包括在局域幺正变换与经典通信辅助的随机局域操作下的分类、多体纠缠的量化，以及通过纠缠见证进行检测的技术。我们还探讨了超图态的其他非经典特性，例如基于稳定子的贝尔型不等式所导出的语境性与真多体非局域性。此外，本文特别关注超图态在纠错编码中的作用，以及其在基于测量的量子计算中的计算资源价值，并分析了其非稳定子特性——通过量子魔力的资源理论度量进行量化。最后，我们回顾了其向高维系统的推广，即量子比特与连续变量情形。

Abstract

Quantum hypergraph states extend the well-studied class of graph states by taking into account multi-qubit interactions through hyperedges. They provide a powerful framework to represent a family of quantum states with genuine multipartite entanglement. In this review, we provide a compact overview of the formal structure, entanglement characteristics, and operational relevance of hypergraph states in quantum information theory. We begin by introducing their mathematical foundations and generalizations of the stabilizer formalism. A central focus is placed on their entanglement properties, including the classification under local unitary (LU) and stochastic local operations with classical communication (SLOCC), the quantification of multipartite entanglement, and detection techniques via entanglement witnesses. We also explore other nonclassical features of hypergraph states, such as contextuality and genuine multipartite nonlocality, derived from stabilizer-based Bell-type inequalities. Additional attention is given to the role of hypergraph states in error correction, and as a computational resource in measurement-based quantum computation (MBQC), and to their non-stabilizer character - quantified via resource-theoretic measures of quantum magic. Finally we review their generalization to higher dimensions, i.e. to qudits and continuous variables.

TL;DR: 该论文研究了如何利用量子纠缠解决现实世界中的决策协调问题，如高频交易和分布式系统，并证明这些量子优势可以通过现有NISQ硬件实现。
摘要翻译

量子传心术是利用量子纠缠解决现实世界中通信受限各方间决策协调问题的概念。通信受限的一种可能原因是延迟约束：某些参与方对必须在生成输出前完成通信，但缺乏足够时间。典型场景包括高频交易和分布式系统。另一原因是隔离性：部分参与方对之间存在通信障碍。典型场景包括救援队搜寻迷途旅行者，以及节点分属竞争企业的网络内部协调。本文对量子传心术的不同应用领域进行了简明综述。研究发现这些现实问题可建模为非局域博弈或其推广形式。文中同时探讨了可能的物理实现方案。量子传心术通过贝尔定理保障量子优势，能直接解决现实问题，例如降低高频交易风险或在自组织网络中高效平衡数据负载。此外，这种量子优势可利用现有含噪声中等规模量子（NISQ）硬件实现物理验证。

Abstract

Quantum telepathy is the concept of using quantum entanglement to solve real-world problems involving decision coordination between parties with restricted communication. One possible reason for this restriction is a latency constraint: some pairs of parties do not have enough time to communicate with each other before they have to produce their outputs. Example scenarios include high frequency trading and distributed systems. Another reason is isolation: for some pairs of parties, there is an obstacle to communication. Example scenarios include locating a stray traveler by a rescue team and coordination within a network where nodes are owned by competing firms. In this paper we give a concise overview of the different application areas of quantum telepathy. We find that these real-world problems can be modeled as nonlocal games or its generalizations. We also discuss possible physical implementations. Quantum telepathy guarantees a quantum advantage via Bell's theorem and can directly solve real-world problems, such as reducing risk in high frequency trading or balancing data loads efficiently in ad hoc networks. Moreover, this quantum advantage can be physically realized with existing NISQ hardware.

Score: 0.0 / 29.0

摘要翻译

Abstract

Quantum batteries are quantum systems that store energy and deliver it on demand, and their practical value hinges on how fast they can be charged. While collective charging protocols and global control are known to enhance charging power, it remains unclear how the battery's internal interaction architecture itself constrains performance. Here we study interacting fermionic batteries whose internal couplings are encoded by a graph adjacency matrix, charged via a simple interaction with an external fermionic device. We prove that the star topology maximises the early time charging power, which proxies the maximal average power - a widely used quantum battery quality metric. We substantiate the result numerically by an exhaustive sweep over all graphs with $N\leq 7$ vertices and by benchmarks against random graph ensembles at larger $N$. Our findings shed light on architecture as a controllable knob for fast charging and motivate hub-and-spoke designs in scalable quantum-battery platforms.

79. Entanglement distillation based on Hamiltonian dynamics FAIL
Score: 0.0 / 29.0
Authors: Zitai Xu, Guoding Liu
Published: 2026-03-11
TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于哈密顿动力学的纠缠蒸馏协议，利用量子信息加扰提高纠缠对保真度，为当前模拟量子平台提供了可扩展的纠缠工程路径。
摘要翻译

高效纠缠提纯是量子信息科学与未来量子网络的核心任务。提纯协议的关键在于量子纠错与探测方案，它们能够提升纠缠对的保真度。传统协议聚焦于数字系统，通常需要复杂的编译电路、高保真度的多量子比特操作以及精密的脉冲级控制，这对近期硬件提出了极高要求。关键在于，量子网络的主流物理平台——囚禁离子与中性原子——均由天然的多体哈密顿量所主导，这些哈密顿量本质上适用于模拟、连续时间演化。利用这些自然动力学比通过精密脉冲级控制来设计数字逻辑更为简单。基于这一实验现实，我们寻求利用固有的模拟能力来实现高效纠缠提纯。在本工作中，我们提出了哈密顿量纠缠提纯协议，该协议利用了在原生哈密顿量下随机时间演化所产生的内在信息置乱效应。我们建立了输出保真度与Out-of-Time-Order Correlators（OTOC，无序时序关联子）之间的定量联系，表明高效的置乱直接意味着良好的提纯性能。由于一般哈密顿量天然就是高效的置乱器，提纯能力普遍存在：希尔伯特空间中几乎所有的哈密顿量都足以实现高保真度提纯。对典型里德堡原子与囚禁离子系统的数值模拟进一步证实，仅利用短程相互作用及当前实验可行的演化时间即可实现稳健的性能。通过规避数字电路控制的复杂性，我们的方法大幅降低了实验要求，为在当前模拟量子平台上进行可扩展的纠缠工程提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract

Efficient entanglement distillation is a central task in quantum information science and future quantum networks. At the core of distillation protocols are the quantum error correction and detection schemes which enhance the fidelity of entangled pairs. Conventional protocols focus on digital systems, which typically require complicated compiled circuits, high-fidelity multi-qubit operations and delicate pulse-level control that impose high demands on near-term hardware. Crucially, the leading physical platforms for quantum networks, trapped ions and neutral atoms, are governed by native many-body Hamiltonians inherently suited for analog, continuous-time evolution. Adopting these natural dynamics is simpler than engineering digital logic via delicate pulse-level control. Motivated by this experimental reality, we seek to leverage the intrinsic analog capabilities for efficient entanglement distillation. In this work, we introduce the Hamiltonian entanglement distillation protocol, which exploits the intrinsic information scrambling generated by random time evolution under native Hamiltonians. We establish a quantitative connection between output fidelity and Out-of-Time-Order Correlators, showing that efficient scrambling directly implies good distillation performance. Since generic Hamiltonians are naturally efficient scramblers, the capability for distillation is ubiquitous: almost all Hamiltonians in the Hilbert space suffice for high-fidelity distillation. Numerical simulations of representative Rydberg-atom and trapped-ion systems further confirm that robust performance could be achieved using only short-range interactions and evolution times feasible in current experiments. By avoiding the complexity of digital circuit control, our approach substantially relaxes experimental requirements, providing a scalable route to entanglement engineering on current analog quantum platforms.
